def all_teams():
    all_teams_dict = {}
    year = 2023
    while year > 1993:
        if year == 2005:
            year -= 1
            continue
        start = f'https://www.hockey-reference.com/leagues/NHL_{year}.html'
        text = requests.get(start).text
        parsed = BeautifulSoup(text, 'html.parser')
        stats_table = parsed.find('div', id='div_standings_EAS')
        if stats_table is None:
            stats_table = parsed.find('div', id='div_standings')
        tbody = stats_table.find('tbody')
        rows_tbody = tbody.find_all('tr')
        thead = stats_table.find('thead')
        rows_thead = thead.find_all('tr')
        east_thead_zoz = []
        east_tbody_zoz = []
        east_team_names = []
        legend = []
        for row in rows_thead:
            cells = row.find_all('th')
            for cell in cells:
                east_thead_zoz.append(cell.text)
                legend.append(cell.get('data-tip'))
        for row in rows_tbody:
            cells = row.find_all('td')
            for cell in cells:
                east_tbody_zoz.append(cell.text)
        for row in rows_tbody:
            cells = row.find_all('th')
            for cell in cells:
                east_team_names.append(cell.text)
        stats_table = parsed.find('div', id='div_standings_WES')
        if stats_table is None:
            stats_table = parsed.find('div', id='div_standings')
        tbody = stats_table.find('tbody')
        rows_tbody = tbody.find_all('tr')
        thead = stats_table.find('thead')
        rows_thead = thead.find_all('tr')
        west_thead_zoz = []
        west_tbody_zoz = []
        west_team_names = []
        for row in rows_thead:
            cells = row.find_all('th')
            for cell in cells:
                west_thead_zoz.append(cell.text)
        for row in rows_tbody:
            cells = row.find_all('td')
            for cell in cells:
                west_tbody_zoz.append(cell.text)
        for row in rows_tbody:
            cells = row.find_all('th')
            for cell in cells:
                west_team_names.append(cell.text)
        if 'Atlantic Division' in east_tbody_zoz:
            east_tbody_zoz.remove('Atlantic Division')
        if 'Metropolitan Division' in east_tbody_zoz:
            east_tbody_zoz.remove('Metropolitan Division')
        if 'Pacific Division' in west_tbody_zoz:
            west_tbody_zoz.remove('Pacific Division')
        if 'Central Division' in west_tbody_zoz:
            west_tbody_zoz.remove('Central Division')

        all_teams_dict[year] = [[east_thead_zoz], [east_tbody_zoz], [east_team_names], [west_thead_zoz], [west_tbody_zoz], [west_team_names], [legend]]
        year -= 1
    print('Team stats crawling finished')
    return all_teams_dict

all_teams_dict = all_teams()

def franchise():
    url = 'https://www.hockey-reference.com/teams/'
    text = requests.get(url).text
    parsed = BeautifulSoup(text, 'html.parser')
    franchise_table = parsed.find('div', id='div_active_franchises')
    tbody = franchise_table.find('tbody')
    rows_tbody = tbody.find_all('tr')
    thead = franchise_table.find('thead')
    rows_thead = thead.find_all('tr')

    thead_zoz = []
    tbody_zoz = []
    legend = []
    for row in rows_thead:
        cells = row.find_all('th')
        for cell in cells:
            thead_zoz.append(cell.text)
            legend.append(cell.get('data-tip'))
    for row in rows_tbody:
        th = row.find('th')
        a_tag = th.find('a')
        if a_tag:
            tbody_zoz.append(a_tag.get_text())
        else:
            tbody_zoz.append(th.text)
        cells = row.find_all('td')
        for cell in cells:
            if cell.text == '':
                tbody_zoz.append('0')
            else:
                tbody_zoz.append(cell.text)
    return legend, thead_zoz, tbody_zoz


franchise_legend, franchise_header, franchise_table = franchise()
In[]:
print(franchise_legend)

franchise_table_split = [franchise_table[i:i + len(franchise_header)] for i in
                         range(0, len(franchise_table), len(franchise_header))]
print(franchise_table_split)

# Writing to the CSV file

    writer = csv.writer(file)
    writer.writerow(franchise_header)  # Write the header
    writer.writerows(franchise_table_split)   # Write multiple rows

print(f"CSV file created at {csv_file_path}.")

def playoffs():
    url = 'https://www.hockey-reference.com/playoffs/'
    text = requests.get(url).text
    parsed = BeautifulSoup(text, 'html.parser')
    franchise_table = parsed.find('div', id='div_playoffs')
    tbody = franchise_table.find('tbody')
    rows_tbody = tbody.find_all('tr')
    thead = franchise_table.find('thead')
    rows_thead = thead.find_all('tr')

    thead_zoz = []
    tbody_zoz = []
    bol_2005 = False
    for row in rows_thead:
        cells = row.find_all('th')
        for cell in cells:
            thead_zoz.append(cell.text)
    for row in rows_tbody:
        th = row.find('th')
        a_tag = th.find('a')
        if a_tag:
            tbody_zoz.append(a_tag.get_text())
        elif not bol_2005:
            tbody_zoz.append('2005')
            bol_2005 = True
        else:
            tbody_zoz.append('1920')
        cells = row.find_all('td')
        for cell in cells:
            tbody_zoz.append(cell.text)
    return thead_zoz, tbody_zoz

playoff_table_header, playoff_table = playoffs()
In[]:
playoff_table_split = [playoff_table[i:i + len(playoff_table_header)] for i in
                range(0, len(playoff_table), len(playoff_table_header))][1:]
print(playoff_table_split)

csv_file_path = 'playoff.csv'

# Writing to the CSV file
with open(csv_file_path, mode='w', newline='') as file:
    writer = csv.writer(file)
    writer.writerow(playoff_table_header)  # Write the header
    writer.writerows(playoff_table_split)   # Write multiple rows

print(f"CSV file created at {csv_file_path}.")

def overtime_goals():
    url = 'https://www.hockey-reference.com/playoffs/overtime-goals.cgi'
    text = requests.get(url).text
    parsed = BeautifulSoup(text, 'html.parser')
    franchise_table = parsed.find('div', id='div_ots')
    tbody = franchise_table.find('tbody')
    rows_tbody = tbody.find_all('tr')
    thead = franchise_table.find('thead')
    rows_thead = thead.find_all('tr')

    thead_zoz = []
    tbody_zoz = []
    for row in rows_thead:
        cells = row.find_all('th')
        for cell in cells:
            thead_zoz.append(cell.text)
    for row in rows_tbody:
        th = row.find('th')
        a_tag = th.find('a')
        tbody_zoz.append(a_tag.get_text())
        cells = row.find_all('td')
        for cell in cells:
            tbody_zoz.append(cell.text)
    updated_headers = [x if x != '' else 'Series Clinch' for x in thead_zoz]
    return updated_headers, tbody_zoz
overtime_goals_header, overtime_goals_table = overtime_goals()
In[]:
print(overtime_goals_header)
print(overtime_goals_table)
overtime_goals_split = [overtime_goals_table[i:i + len(overtime_goals_header)] for i in
               range(0, len(overtime_goals_table), len(overtime_goals_header))]
print(overtime_goals_split)

csv_file_path = 'overtime.csv'

# Writing to the CSV file
with open(csv_file_path, mode='w', newline='') as file:
    writer = csv.writer(file)
    writer.writerow(overtime_goals_header)  # Write the header
    writer.writerows(overtime_goals_split)   # Write multiple rows

print(f"CSV file created at {csv_file_path}.")
